
-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
begin

 ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-09-28 | 01) add call to scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes
   ------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   truncate table clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log;
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_a100_check_cnt_rows();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_c1000_check_file_history();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_f000_check_valid_tpa_in();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_g000_verify_claim_list();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_h000_rtrim();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim();
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes();

  

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver() TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver() TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver() TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_0000_driver() TO iicsuser;
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text)

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text);

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(
	p_verify_id text,
	p_sql text)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id_desc   varchar;
declare v_sql              varchar;
declare v_nbr_of_errors    bigint;
declare v_retired          boolean;         
begin
 

   
   -------------------------------
   -------------------------------
   select verify_id_desc
         ,retired
   into v_verify_id_desc 
       ,v_retired
   from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_id 
   where 1         = 1
    and  verify_id = p_verify_id;
   
   if v_retired = true then
      return;
   end if;
   
   if v_verify_id_desc is null then
      raise NOTICE 'Z100 - No description for verify_id of % found in table clmscc_verify.scc_verify_id ', p_verify_id ;
      return;
   end if;
   v_nbr_of_errors = 0;

   v_sql = 'select count(*) from (' || p_sql || ' ) x;';
   

   execute v_sql into v_nbr_of_errors;

   insert into clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log 
   (
        verify_id
       ,verify_id_desc
       ,nbr_of_errors
       ,sql_used
   ) 
   select p_verify_id
        ,v_verify_id_desc
        ,v_nbr_of_errors
        ,v_sql 
   where 1 = 1;
 
end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text)
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text) TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text) TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text) TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text) TO qa_ete1;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(text, text) TO iicsuser;

             clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data       
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A470';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select end_of_record_indicator 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data
                   except
                       select clmscc_lku.f_end_of_record_ind_asterisk()
                  $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
         
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
       A473  invalid end_of_record_indicator_cna in table:
             clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data       
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A473';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select end_of_record_indicator_cna 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data
                   except
                       select clmscc_lku.f_end_of_record_ind_asterisk()
                  $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*   
       A476  invalid end_of_record_indicator in table:
             clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_stat_code_combined       
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A476';
   v_sql       = $$

                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_stat_code_combined
                   except
                       select clmscc_lku.f_end_of_record_ind_asterisk()
                  $$;

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ---  A500   verify we have no additional database tables.
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A500';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                      select table_schema
                             ,table_name
                       from information_schema.tables 
                       where 1          = 1
                        and table_schema in  
                                            (
                                              'clmscc_lku'
                                             ,'clmscc_mgmt'

                   except (

                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_administrator'

                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_error_cd'

                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_to_email'
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_booking_period'

                       union all select 'clmscc_verify'               ,'scc_verify_log'  
                          )
                  $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ---  A502   verify we have the required list of database tables
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A502';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                      (          select 'clmscc_lku'      as schema   ,'scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd'           as table_name
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_administrator'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_amount_type_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_booked_conv'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_booking_type_cd'

                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_claim_suffix_list_conv'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_claim_totals_merlin_ceded'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_claim_totals_procede'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_email_msg_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_error_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_file_name_to_administrator'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_file_type_cd'

                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_reins_treaty_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_reins_type_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_scc_close'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_scc_cycle_type_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_scc_record_id'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_source_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_to_email'
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_booking_period'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_broker_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_contract_layer_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_coverage_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_file_type_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_reinsurer_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_tpa_treaty_fac_cd'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_lku'                  ,'scc_lku_truncate_table_list'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'flyway_schema_history'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_act_claim_xfer'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_booked'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_file_inbound_outbound_history'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_recycle'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_recycle_stat_code'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt'                 ,'scc_valid_tpa_in'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_inbound_tmp_claim_stat_code'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_file_inbound_outbound_history'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_enstar'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_enstar_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_scc_close'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_scc_close_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_in_tpa'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_out_booked'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_out_booked_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_out_tpa_error_cna_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_out_tpa_error_ctl'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_booked'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_claim_itd_totals'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_claim_list'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_claim_stat_code'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_claims_amounts'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_stat_code_combined'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_stat_code_reentry'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_stat_code_reverse'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_tpa_combined'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'              ,'scc_tmp_tpa_current'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_verify'               ,'scc_verify_id'  
                       union all select 'clmscc_verify'               ,'scc_verify_log'  
                      )
                   except  
                       select table_schema
                             ,table_name
                       from information_schema.tables 
                       where 1          = 1
                        and table_schema in  
                                            (
                                              'clmscc_lku'
                                             ,'clmscc_mgmt'
                                             ,'clmscc_staging'
                                             ,'clmscc_verify'
                                            )
                $$;
   
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ---  A504   verify database clmscc_db has all the required schemas
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A504';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        (
                                 select 'clmscc_lku'      as schema    
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt' 
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'   
                       union all select 'clmscc_verify'   
                       union all select 'information_schema'  
                       union all select 'pg_catalog'  
                       union all select 'public'  
                          )
                   except 
                      select schema_name from information_schema.schemata where catalog_name = 'clmscc_db' 
                 $$;
   
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ---  A506   verify database clmscc_db does not have any extra schemas
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'A506';
   v_sql       = $$
                      select schema_name from information_schema.schemata where catalog_name = 'clmscc_db' 
                   except (
                                 select 'clmscc_lku'      as schema    
                       union all select 'clmscc_mgmt' 
                       union all select 'clmscc_staging'   
                       union all select 'clmscc_verify'   
                       union all select 'information_schema'  
                       union all select 'pg_catalog'  
                       union all select 'public'  
                          )   
                 $$;
   
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   return;   

end; 
$BODY$;

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;

begin
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-08-25 | 01) Add Edit B300
--               |     verify scc_record of 
--               |     clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl 
--               |     is formatted correctly   
--               | 02) Retire B160 - Normal Run should not have any data
   ------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'B%';

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B100   totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer                                                   
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select cycle_dt 
                             ,count(*)  as total_nbr_of_rows 
                       from  clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer        
                       group by cycle_dt
                   except
                       select cycle_dt 
                             ,total_nbr_of_rows 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer_ctl
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B110    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg                                                
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select cycle_dt 
                             ,count(*)  as total_nbr_of_rows 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg     
                       group by cycle_dt
                   except
                       select cycle_dt 
                             ,total_nbr_of_rows 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg_ctl
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B120    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar                                                           
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B120';
   v_sql       = $$
                       select count(*)                                                   as total_number_of_rows
                             ,sum(cast(paid_loss_amt                         as money))  as total_paid_loss
                             ,sum(cast(paid_lae_amt                          as money))  as total_paid_lae
                             ,sum(cast(outstanding_loss_amt                  as money))  as total_outstanding_loss
                             ,sum(cast(outstanding_lae_amt                   as money))  as total_outstanding_lae
                             ,sum(cast(period_end_outstanding_loss_amt       as money))  as total_period_end_outstanding_loss
                             ,sum(cast(period_end_outstanding_lae_amt        as money))  as total_period_end_outstanding_lae
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar
                   except
                       select cast(total_number_of_rows                      as bigint)  as total_number_of_rows
                             ,cast(total_paid_loss                           as money )  as total_paid_loss
                             ,cast(total_paid_lae                            as money )  as total_paid_lae
                             ,cast(total_outstanding_loss                    as money )  as total_outstanding_loss
                             ,cast(total_outstanding_lae                     as money )  as total_outstanding_lae
                             ,cast(total_period_end_outstanding_loss         as money )  as total_period_end_outstanding_loss
                             ,cast(total_period_end_outstanding_lae          as money )  as total_period_end_outstanding_lae
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar_ctl   
                $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B130    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close                                                        
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B130';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select cycle_dt                                                          
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,count(*)                           as total_nbr_of_rows
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close
                       group by cycle_dt
                               ,scc_close_yyyymm
                   except
                       select cycle_dt
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,total_nbr_of_rows
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close_ctl
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B140    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa                                                              
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B140';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select count(*)                             as tpa_total_nbr_of_rows
                             ,sum(tpa_paid_loss_amt              ) as tpa_total_paid_loss_amt
                             ,sum(tpa_paid_lae_amt               ) as tpa_total_paid_lae_amt
                             ,sum(tpa_outstanding_loss_amt       ) as tpa_total_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,sum(tpa_outstanding_lae_amt        ) as tpa_total_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,sum(tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt) as tpa_total_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,sum(tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt ) as tpa_total_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa
                   except
                       select tpa_total_nbr_of_rows
                             ,tpa_total_paid_loss_amt
                             ,tpa_total_paid_lae_amt
                             ,tpa_total_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,tpa_total_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,tpa_total_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,tpa_total_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa_ctl
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
  
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B150    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked                                                          
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'B150';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,count(*)                         as scc_nbr_of_records
                             ,sum(scc_reserve_amt)             as scc_total_reserve_amt
                             ,sum(scc_loss_amt)                as scc_total_loss_amt
                             ,sum(scc_expense_amt)             as scc_total_expense_amt
                             ,sum(scc_salvage_subro_amt)       as scc_total_salvage_subro_amt
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                       group by scc_close_yyyymm
                   except
                       select scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,scc_nbr_of_records
                             ,scc_total_reserve_amt
                             ,scc_total_loss_amt
                             ,scc_total_expense_amt
                             ,scc_total_salvage_subro_amt
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl
                       where 1 = 1
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   /*
        B160    totals not match between 
               clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_cna_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_ctl 
               and clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data    
   */   
   ------------------------------------------------------
    v_verify_id = 'B160';
    v_sql       = $$ 
                       select file_name_out
                             ,total_nbr_of_rows
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_cna_ctl
                   except 
                          (
                                select file_name_out
                                      ,count(*)
                                from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_ctl
                                group by file_name_out
                                union all
                                select file_name_out
                                      ,count(*)
                                from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_tpa_error_data
                                group by file_name_out 
                         )
                 $$;
   ----call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --
   -- B300   verify scc_record of clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl 
   --        is formatted correctly totals not match between 
   --
   ------------------------------------------------------
    v_verify_id = 'B300';
    v_sql       = $$ 
                                select           scc_close_yyyymm
                                       || '|' || scc_nbr_of_records
                                       || '|' || scc_total_reserve_amt
                                       || '|' || scc_total_loss_amt
                                       || '|' || scc_total_expense_amt
                                       || '|' || scc_total_salvage_subro_amt
                                       || '|' || end_of_record_indicator
                                from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl
                                where 1 = 1
                   except
                                select scc_record
                                from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked_ctl
                                where 1 = 1
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   return;

  

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_b100_ctl_and_data() TO PUBLIC;

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C470 Every enstar_reacct_5042*.ctl file from 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                       
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C470';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.ctl' as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'enstar_reacct_5042%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C480 Every enstar_reacct_5042*.touch file from 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C480';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.touch'  as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'enstar_reacct_5042%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   ---------------call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   -----------------------------------------------------------------
   --- scc_1057
   ----------------------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C490 Every scc_1057*.dat file from 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C490';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.dat' as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history

                 $$;

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C500 Every scc_1057*.ctl file from 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C500';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.ctl' as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'scc_1057%'

                 $$;

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C510 Every scc_1057*.touch file from 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history should be
   --       in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C510';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.touch'  as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'scc_1057%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   --------------call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   -----------------------------------------------------------------
   --- scc_proper_booking_period
   ----------------------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C520 Every scc_proper_booking_period*.dat file 
   --       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------

   v_sql       = $$

                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'scc_proper_booking_period%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C530 Every scc_proper_booking_period*.ctl file 
   --       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C530';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.ctl' as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'scc_proper_booking_period%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  C540 Every scc_proper_booking_period*.touch file 
   --       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history 
   --       should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history                                        
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'C540';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select split_part(file_name_in_out,'.', 1) || '.touch'  as file_name_in_out
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                        where file_name_in_out like 'scc_proper_booking_period%' 
                   except
                        select file_name_in_out from clmscc_mgmt.scc_file_inbound_outbound_history
                 $$;
 

   --------------call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   return;

  

end;

	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$

declare v_sql            varchar;
begin

   ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-08-30 | 01) Change Edit D157 - Number of rows in clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked should match the sum of rows in scc_tmp_booked
   ------------------------------------------------
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'D%';

   
   
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D100 - clmscc_lku.scc_lku_booked_conv 
   --        should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------

                   except

                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D105  count(*) from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_booked_conv 
   --       should match startup records in 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D105';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select count(*)
                           from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_booked_conv
                   except 
                           select count(*)
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked

                $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D110 - clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked 
   --        should be in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select scc_close_yyyymm
                                , administrator
                                , tpa_claim_nbr
                                , cna_seq_nbr
                                , booking_type_cd
                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd

                                , cna_claim_nbr

                                , catastrophe_cd

                                , category_cd

                   except

                                , administrator

                                , cna_seq_nbr

                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd

                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D115 Number of rows in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
   --      should match for the current booking period        
   ------------------------------------------------------ 
   v_verify_id = 'D115';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                             select count(*) 
                             from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                   except 
                             select count(*) 
                             from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked              b 
                                 ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                             where b.scc_close_yyyymm = c.scc_close_yyyymm
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D120 - Build of scc_record in 
   --        clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D120';
   v_sql       = $$
                             select                  id                                              
                                                    ,scc_source_cd                                 
                                           || '|' || company_cd                                      
                                           || '|' || scc_record_id                                   
                                           || '|' || cna_claim_nbr  ||   cna_suffix_cd               
                                           || '|' || policy_number                                   
                                           || '|' || policy_eff_dt_str                               
                                           || '|' || loss_dt_str                                     
                                           || '|' || notice_dt_str                                 
                                           || '|' || premium_state_cd                                
                                           || '|' || product_responsibility_cd  || policy_type_cd    
                                           || '|' || major_line_cd                                   
                                           || '|' || subline_cd                                      
                                           || '|' || cause_of_loss_cd                                
                                           || '|' || ''                      -- scc_filler_01                    
                                           || '|' || catastrophe_cd                                  
                                           || '|' || rating_method_cd                                
                                           || '|' || category_cd                                     
                                           || '|' || reinsurer_cd                                    
                                           || '|' ||  ''                        -- scc_filler_02                    
                                           || '|' || reins_type_cd                                
                                           || '|' || reins_treaty_cd                              
                                           || '|' || branch_cd                                    
                                           || '|' || producer_cd                                   
                                           || '|' || case when indemnity_medical_ind is null then '' else indemnity_medical_ind end  
                                           || '|' || trunc(scc_reserve_amt)                                       
                                           || '|' || scc_loss_amt                                                 
                                           || '|' || scc_expense_amt                                              
                                           || '|' || scc_salvage_subro_amt                                        
                                           || '|' || adjusting_location_cd                                         
                                           || '|' || end_of_record_indicator                                      
                             from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                             where 1          = 1
                   except 
                             select id
                                   ,scc_record
                             from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                             where 1           = 1
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D130 - Build of scc_record in 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D130';
   v_sql       = $$        
                            select                 id                                                
                                                 ,scc_source_cd                                
                                      || '|'  ||  company_cd                                      
                                      || '|'  ||  scc_record_id                                   
                                      || '|'  ||  cna_claim_nbr              || cna_suffix_cd               
                                      || '|'  ||  policy_number                                   
                                      || '|'  ||  policy_eff_dt_str                               
                                      || '|'  ||  loss_dt_str

                                      || '|'  ||  premium_state_cd

                                      || '|'  ||  subline_cd                                      
                                      || '|'  ||  cause_of_loss_cd                                
                                      || '|'  ||  ''                                              -- scc_filler_01                    
                                      || '|'  ||  catastrophe_cd                                 
                                      || '|'  ||  rating_method_cd                               
                                      || '|'  ||  category_cd                                    
                                      || '|'  ||  reinsurer_cd                                   
                                      || '|'  || ''                                              -- scc_filler_02                    
                                      || '|'  ||  reins_type_cd                                  
                                      || '|'  ||  reins_treaty_cd                              
                                      || '|'  ||  branch_cd                                    
                                      || '|'  ||  producer_cd                                  
                                      || '|'  ||  case when indemnity_medical_ind is null then '' else indemnity_medical_ind end  
                                      || '|'  ||  trunc(scc_reserve_amt)                                       
                                      || '|'  ||  scc_loss_amt                                                 
                                      || '|'  ||  scc_expense_amt                                              
                                      || '|'  ||  scc_salvage_subro_amt                                        
                                      || '|'  ||  adjusting_location_cd                                         
                                      || '|'  ||  end_of_record_indicator                                      
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
                           where 1           = 1
                            and  ind_startup = false
                   except 
                           select id
                                 ,scc_record
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
                           where 1           = 1
                            and  ind_startup = false
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D140 - Count between 
   --        clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked and 
   --        clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked should equal
   ------------------------------------------------------

                   except

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D150 - Verify clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked 
   --        using Move clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D150';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select scc_close_yyyymm
                                , administrator
                                , tpa_claim_nbr
                                , cna_seq_nbr
                                , booking_type_cd
                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd
                                , scc_record_id
                                , cna_claim_nbr
                                , cna_suffix_cd

                                , policy_eff_dt_str

                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                   except
                           select scc_close_yyyymm
                                , administrator

                                , cna_seq_nbr
                                , booking_type_cd
                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd
                                , scc_record_id

   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  D155 Number of rows in 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked and 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked should match
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D155';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select count(*)
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked 
                   except
                           select count(*) 
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   --  D157 Number of rows in 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked should match the 
   --       number of rows 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D157';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select count(*)
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                   except
                           select sum(x.nbr)
                           from (
                                      select count(*) as nbr
                                      from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked
                                ) x
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D160 - Verify clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked 
   --        using Move clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D160';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select scc_close_yyyymm
                                , administrator
                                , tpa_claim_nbr
                                , cna_seq_nbr
                                , booking_type_cd
                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd
                                , scc_record_id
                                , cna_claim_nbr
                                , cna_suffix_cd
                                , policy_number
                                , policy_eff_dt_str
                                , loss_dt_str
                                , notice_dt_str
                                , premium_state_cd
                                , product_responsibility_cd
                                , policy_type_cd
                                , major_line_cd
                                , subline_cd
                                , cause_of_loss_cd
                                , scc_filler_01
                                , catastrophe_cd
                                , rating_method_cd
                                , category_cd
                                , reinsurer_cd
                                , scc_filler_02
                                , reins_type_cd
                                , reins_treaty_cd
                                , branch_cd
                                , producer_cd
                                , indemnity_medical_ind
                                , adjusting_location_cd
                                , amount_type_cd
                                , amount
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_booked 
                   except
                           select scc_close_yyyymm
                                , administrator
                                , tpa_claim_nbr
                                , cna_seq_nbr
                                , booking_type_cd
                                , scc_source_cd
                                , company_cd
                                , scc_record_id
                                , cna_claim_nbr
                                , cna_suffix_cd
                                , policy_number
                                , policy_eff_dt_str
                                , loss_dt_str
                                , notice_dt_str
                                , premium_state_cd
                                , product_responsibility_cd
                                , policy_type_cd
                                , major_line_cd
                                , subline_cd
                                , cause_of_loss_cd
                                , scc_filler_01
                                , catastrophe_cd
                                , rating_method_cd
                                , category_cd
                                , reinsurer_cd
                                , scc_filler_02
                                , reins_type_cd
                                , reins_treaty_cd
                                , branch_cd
                                , producer_cd
                                , indemnity_medical_ind
                                , adjusting_location_cd
                                , amount_type_cd
                                , amount
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D170 - Verify stat codes in 
   --        clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked for 
   --        booking_type is regular or reentry
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D170';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select  administrator
                                 , tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_suffix_cd
                                 , company_cd
                                 , policy_number
                                 , policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , loss_dt_str
                                 , notice_dt_str
                                 , premium_state_cd
                                 , product_responsibility_cd
                                 , policy_type_cd
                                 , major_line_cd
                                 , subline_cd
                                 , cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , catastrophe_cd
                                 , rating_method_cd
                                 , branch_cd
                                 , producer_cd
                                 , adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_regular()
                            or   booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry()
                   except
                           select  administrator
                                 , tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_suffix_cd
                                 , company_cd
                                 , policy_number
                                 , policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , loss_dt_str
                                 , notice_dt_str
                                 , premium_state_cd
                                 , product_responsibility_cd
                                 , policy_type_cd
                                 , major_line_cd
                                 , subline_cd
                                 , cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , catastrophe_cd
                                 , rating_method_cd
                                 , branch_cd
                                 , producer_cd
                                 , adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_stat_code                 
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D180 - Verify stat codes in clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked match clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_stat_code from regular and reentry 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D180';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                           select  administrator
                                 , tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_suffix_cd
                                 , company_cd
                                 , policy_number
                                 , policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , loss_dt_str
                                 , notice_dt_str
                                 , premium_state_cd
                                 , product_responsibility_cd
                                 , policy_type_cd
                                 , major_line_cd
                                 , subline_cd
                                 , cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , catastrophe_cd
                                 , rating_method_cd
                                 , branch_cd
                                 , producer_cd
                                 , adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_regular()
                            or   booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry()
                   except
                           select  administrator
                                 , tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_suffix_cd
                                 , company_cd
                                 , policy_number
                                 , policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , loss_dt_str
                                 , notice_dt_str
                                 , premium_state_cd
                                 , product_responsibility_cd
                                 , policy_type_cd
                                 , major_line_cd
                                 , subline_cd
                                 , cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , catastrophe_cd
                                 , rating_method_cd
                                 , branch_cd
                                 , producer_cd
                                 , adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_stat_code   
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D190 - Verify stat codes in 
   --        clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked where the 
   --        booking_type is regular or reentry are in the CFI 
   --        table clmscc_staging.scc_inbound_tmp_claim_stat_code
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D190';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select  administrator
                                 , tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_claim_nbr
                                 , cna_suffix_cd
                                 , company_cd
                                 , policy_number
                                 , policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , loss_dt_str
                                 , notice_dt_str
                                 , premium_state_cd
                                 , product_responsibility_cd
                                 , policy_type_cd
                                 , major_line_cd
                                 , subline_cd
                                 , cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , catastrophe_cd
                                 , rating_method_cd
                                 , branch_cd
                                 , producer_cd
                                 , adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_out_booked
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_regular()
                            or   booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry()
                   except
                           select  s.administrator
                                 , s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                 , s.cna_claim_nbr
                                 , s.cna_suffix_cd
                                 , s.company_cd
                                 , s.policy_number
                                 , s.policy_eff_dt_str
                                 , s.loss_dt_str
                                 , x.notice_dt
                                 , s.premium_state_cd
                                 , s.product_responsibility_cd
                                 , s.policy_type_cd
                                 , s.major_line_cd
                                 , s.subline_cd
                                 , s.cause_of_loss_cd
                                 , s.catastrophe_cd
                                 , s.rating_method_cd
                                 , s.branch_cd
                                 , s.producer_cd
                                 , s.adjusting_location_cd
                           from clmscc_staging.scc_inbound_tmp_claim_stat_code s
                               ,clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer                 x
                           where 1 = 1
                            and  s.tpa_claim_nbr = x.tpa_claim_nbr
                            and  s.cna_claim_nbr = x.cna_claim_nbr
                            and  s.cna_suffix_cd = x.cna_suffix_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D700 - Verify scc_close_yyyymm from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using clmscc_lku.scc_lku_scc_close
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D700';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_close_yyyymm from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select scc_close_yyyymm from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_scc_close
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D702 - Verify administrator from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked  using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D702';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select administrator from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select administrator from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D704 - Verify  administrator ,tpa_claim_nbr 
   --        ,cna_seq_nbr ,cna_claim_nbr ,cna_suffix_cd 
   --        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D704';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select administrator ,tpa_claim_nbr ,cna_seq_nbr ,cna_claim_nbr ,cna_suffix_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select administrator ,tpa_claim_nbr ,cna_seq_nbr ,cna_claim_nbr ,cna_suffix_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D706 - Verify booking_type_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_booking_type_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D706';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select booking_type_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select booking_type_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_booking_type_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D708 - Verify scc_source_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_source_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D708';
   v_sql       = $$        select scc_source_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select scc_source_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_source_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D710 - Verify administrator, scc_source_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_source_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D710';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select administrator, scc_source_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select administrator, scc_source_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_source_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D712 - Verify scc_record_id from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_scc_record_id
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D712';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_record_id from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select scc_record_id from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_scc_record_id
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D714 - Verify scc_filler_01 from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked is null
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D714';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_filler_01 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select null           
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D716 - Verify category_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked is a 4 or 5 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D716';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select category_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           (select '4' union select '5')
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D718 - Verify scc_filler_02 from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked is null
    ------------------------------------------------------ 
   v_verify_id = 'D718';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_filler_02 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select null          
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D720 - Verify reinsurer_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_reinsurer_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D720';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select reinsurer_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked               where reins_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_reins_type_cd_facultative()
                   except 
                           select reinsurer_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_reinsurer_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D722 - reins_type_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
   --        using clmscc_lku.scc_lku_reins_type_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D722';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select reins_type_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked    
                   except 
                           select reins_type_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_reins_type_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D724 - Verify reins_treaty_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_reins_treaty_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D724';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select reins_treaty_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked            where reins_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_reins_type_cd_treaty()
                   except 
                           select reins_treaty_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_reins_treaty_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D726- Verify reinsurer_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked is 0000 when treaty 
   --        record
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D726';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select reinsurer_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked               where reins_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_reins_type_cd_treaty()
                   except 
                           select clmscc_lku.f_reins_treaty_cd_default()
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D728 - Verify reins_treaty_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked is 0000 when 
   --        facultative record
   ------------------------------------------------------  
   v_verify_id = 'D728';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select reins_treaty_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked            where reins_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_reins_type_cd_facultative()
                   except 
                           select clmscc_lku.f_reins_treaty_cd_default() 
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D730 - Verify administrator ,adjusting_location_cd 
   --        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D730';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select administrator ,adjusting_location_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked            
                   except 
                           select administrator ,adjusting_location_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd 
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D732 - Verify amount_type_cd from 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked using 
   --        clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D732';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select amount_type_cd from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                   except 
                           select amount_type_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D734 - Verify scc_reserve_amt in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D734';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_reserve_amt ,scc_loss_amt ,scc_expense_amt ,scc_salvage_subro_amt ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                   except 
                           select amount          ,0.00         ,0.00            ,0.00                  ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D736 - Verify scc_loss_amt in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D736';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_reserve_amt ,scc_loss_amt ,scc_expense_amt ,scc_salvage_subro_amt ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_lae()
                   except 
                           select 0.00          ,0.00         ,amount            ,0.00                  ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_lae()
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D738 - Verify scc_expense_amt in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D738';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_reserve_amt ,scc_loss_amt ,scc_expense_amt ,scc_salvage_subro_amt ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_paid()
                   except 
                           select 0.00         ,amount        ,0.00            ,0.00                  ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_paid()
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D740 - Verify scc_salvage_subro_amt in 
   --        clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D740';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_reserve_amt ,scc_loss_amt ,scc_expense_amt ,scc_salvage_subro_amt ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_salvage()
                   except 
                           select 0.00           ,0.00         ,0.00            ,amount                  ,amount from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked where amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_salvage()
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D745 - verify reverse and reentry net to zero in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D745';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select scc_close_yyyymm, administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_seq_nbr, amount_type_cd, sum(amount)  
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry() 
                              or booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reverse()
                           group by scc_close_yyyymm, administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_seq_nbr, amount_type_cd
                   except 
                           select scc_close_yyyymm, administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_seq_nbr, amount_type_cd, sum(0)
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry() 
                             or booking_type_cd  = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reverse()
                           group by scc_close_yyyymm, administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_seq_nbr, amount_type_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- D750 - verify not doing reversal and reentry on as of money in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'D750';
   v_sql       = $$
                           select amount_type_cd 
                           from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked 
                           where booking_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reentry() 
                            or   booking_type_cd  = clmscc_lku.f_booking_type_cd_reverse()
                   except 
                           select amount_type_cd from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd where ind_as_of = false
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   return;

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked() TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked() TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked() TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_d000_booked() TO iicsuser;
