-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;

begin
 

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'E%';

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- E100  verify clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer 
   --       is in clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer               
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'E100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select tpa_claim_nbr
                            , cna_claim_nbr
                            , cna_suffix_cd
                            , catastrophe_cd_act
                            , notice_dt  
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_claim_xfer
                   except
                       select tpa_claim_nbr
                            , cna_claim_nbr
                            , cna_suffix_cd
                            , catastrophe_cd_act
                            , notice_dt  
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

  return;

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer() TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer() TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer() TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer() TO qa_ete1;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_e000_check_claim_xfer() TO iicsuser;


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_f000_check_valid_tpa_in()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_f000_check_valid_tpa_in();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_f000_check_valid_tpa_in(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;
declare v_count_current  bigint;
begin

   ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-08-30 | 01) Add Edit F200 - verify tpa_close_yyyymm is caculated correctly in clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
   ------------------------------------------------
  

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'F%';

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F100  verify contract information    
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F100';
   v_sql       = $$
                       select administrator
                            , contract_cd
                            , contract_underwriting_year
                            , contract_layer_cd
                            , contract_layer_number
                            , contract_type_cd
                            , contract_type_cd_desc
                            , contract_cd_desc
                            , contract_layer_cd_desc  
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                   except
                       select administrator
                            , contract_cd
                            , contract_underwriting_year
                            , contract_layer_cd
                            , contract_layer_number
                            , contract_type_cd
                            , contract_type_cd_desc
                            , contract_cd_desc
                            , contract_layer_cd_desc  
                       from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_contract_layer_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F110  verify broker information          
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_broker_cd 
                             ,tpa_broker_name
                             ,broker_cd
                             ,broker_name 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_broker_cd 
                             ,tpa_broker_name
                             ,broker_cd
                             ,broker_name 
                       from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_broker_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F120 verify reinsurer information               
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F120';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_reinsurer_cd 
                             ,tpa_reinsurer_name
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,reinsurer_name 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_reinsurer_cd 
                             ,tpa_reinsurer_name
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,reinsurer_name 
                       from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_reinsurer_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F130  verify suffix information in  
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in                
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F130';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_coverage_cd 
                             ,tpa_coverage_cd_desc
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_coverage_cd 
                             ,tpa_coverage_cd_desc
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_coverage_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F140  verify scc amounts in 
   --       clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in                 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F140';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select id
                            , tpa_paid_loss_amt 
                            , tpa_paid_lae_amt 
                            , 0.00                  
                            , tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt + tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                   except
                       select id
                            , scc_loss_amt      
                            , scc_expense_amt  
                            , scc_salvage_subro_amt 
                            , scc_reserve_amt_money    
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F150  verify data from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa 
   --       is in clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in              
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F150';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                           , tpa_file_type_cd
                           , tpa_file_name
                           , tpa_file_record_nbr
                           , tpa_run_dt
                           , tpa_starting_dt
                           , tpa_ending_dt
                           , tpa_treaty_fac_cd
                           , tpa_contract_layer_cd
                           , tpa_broker_cd
                           , tpa_reinsurer_cd
                           , tpa_claim_nbr
                           , tpa_policy_nbr
                           , tpa_policy_eff_dt
                           , tpa_coverage_cd
                           , tpa_paid_loss_amt
                           , tpa_paid_lae_amt
                           , tpa_outstanding_loss_amt
                           , tpa_outstanding_lae_amt
                           , tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                           , tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                           , tpa_close_yyyymm
                           , scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                           , contract_cd
                           , contract_underwriting_year
                           , contract_layer_cd
                           , contract_layer_number
                           , contract_type_cd
                           , contract_type_cd_desc
                           , contract_cd_desc
                           , contract_layer_cd_desc
                           , tpa_broker_name
                           , broker_cd
                           , broker_name
                           , tpa_reinsurer_name
                           , reinsurer_cd
                           , reinsurer_name
                           , tpa_coverage_cd_desc
                           , cna_suffix_cd
                           , scc_loss_amt
                           , scc_expense_amt
                           , scc_salvage_subro_amt
                           , scc_reserve_amt_money
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa
                   except
                       select administrator
                           , tpa_file_type_cd
                           , tpa_file_name
                           , tpa_file_record_nbr
                           , tpa_run_dt
                           , tpa_starting_dt
                           , tpa_ending_dt
                           , tpa_treaty_fac_cd
                           , tpa_contract_layer_cd
                           , tpa_broker_cd
                           , tpa_reinsurer_cd
                           , tpa_claim_nbr
                           , tpa_policy_nbr
                           , tpa_policy_eff_dt
                           , tpa_coverage_cd
                           , tpa_paid_loss_amt
                           , tpa_paid_lae_amt
                           , tpa_outstanding_loss_amt
                           , tpa_outstanding_lae_amt
                           , tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                           , tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                           , tpa_close_yyyymm
                           , scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                           , contract_cd
                           , contract_underwriting_year
                           , contract_layer_cd
                           , contract_layer_number
                           , contract_type_cd
                           , contract_type_cd_desc
                           , contract_cd_desc
                           , contract_layer_cd_desc
                           , tpa_broker_name
                           , broker_cd
                           , broker_name
                           , tpa_reinsurer_name
                           , reinsurer_cd
                           , reinsurer_name
                           , tpa_coverage_cd_desc
                           , cna_suffix_cd
                           , scc_loss_amt
                           , scc_expense_amt
                           , scc_salvage_subro_amt
                           , scc_reserve_amt_money
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
      ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F160  verify data from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar 
   --       is in clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa             
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F160';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select clmscc_lku.f_administrator_enstar()                             as administrator
                             ,txn_seq_no                                                      as tpa_file_record_nbr
                             ,tpa_file_name                                                   as tpa_file_name
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_date_from_yyyy_mm_dd_ddl(run_date                ) as tpa_run_dt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_date_from_yyyy_mm_dd_ddl(starting_date           ) as tpa_starting_dt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_date_from_yyyy_mm_dd_ddl(ending_date             ) as tpa_ending_dt
                             ,treaty_fac                                                      as tpa_treaty_fac_cd
                             ,contract_no                                                     as tpa_contract_layer_cd
                             ,broker_number                                                   as tpa_broker_cd
                             ,reinsurer_number                                                as tpa_reinsurer_cd
                             ,claim_no                                                        as tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,policy_number                                                   as tpa_policy_nbr
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_date_from_yyyy_mm_dd_ddl(policy_eff              ) as tpa_policy_eff_dt
                             ,coverage                                                        as tpa_coverage_cd
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(paid_loss_amt                  ) as tpa_paid_loss_amt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(paid_lae_amt                   ) as tpa_paid_lae_amt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(outstanding_loss_amt           ) as tpa_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(outstanding_lae_amt            ) as tpa_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(period_end_outstanding_loss_amt) as tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_money_from_string(period_end_outstanding_lae_amt ) as tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,end_of_record_indicator                                         as tpa_end_of_record_indicator
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_enstar
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_file_record_nbr
                             ,tpa_file_name
                             ,tpa_run_dt
                             ,tpa_starting_dt
                             ,tpa_ending_dt
                             ,tpa_treaty_fac_cd
                             ,tpa_contract_layer_cd
                             ,tpa_broker_cd
                             ,tpa_reinsurer_cd
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,tpa_policy_nbr
                             ,tpa_policy_eff_dt
                             ,tpa_coverage_cd
                             ,cast(tpa_paid_loss_amt               as money) as tpa_paid_loss_amt
                             ,cast(tpa_paid_lae_amt                as money) as tpa_paid_lae_amt
                             ,cast(tpa_outstanding_loss_amt        as money) as tpa_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,cast(tpa_outstanding_lae_amt         as money) as tpa_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,cast(tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt as money) as tpa_ending_outstanding_loss_amt
                             ,cast(tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt  as money) as tpa_ending_outstanding_lae_amt
                             ,tpa_end_of_record_indicator
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
      ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F170  verify administrator,tpa_file_type_cd,tpa_close_yyyymm 
   --       and scc_close_yyyymm_proposed in clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa    
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F170';
   v_sql       = $$  
                       select id
                             ,administrator
                             ,tpa_file_type_cd
                             ,tpa_close_yyyymm
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa                   
                   except
                       select id
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_administrator_enstar()                                                as administrator
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_file_type_cd_data()                                                   as tpa_file_type_cd
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_yyyymm_from_date(tpa_ending_dt)                                       as tpa_close_yyyymm
                             ,clmscc_lku.f_month_add_from_yyyymm(clmscc_lku.f_yyyymm_from_date(tpa_ending_dt),2) as scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_tpa
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
      ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F180  verify clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined when we have 
   --       data for the current accounting period 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F180';
   v_sql       = $$  
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                   except
                       select x.administrator  
                             ,x.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed   
                             ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                             ,x.reinsurer_cd
                             ,x.amount_type_cd
                             ,sum((x.amount * lku.multiplier_scc))                                            as amount
                       from (
                                 select s.administrator 
                                       ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed 
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr 
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd  
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd   
                                       ,clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()                   as amount_type_cd    
                                       ,round(cast(sum(scc_reserve_amt_money) as numeric),0) as amount 
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s   
                                     ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c  
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                 union all
                                 select s.administrator
                                       ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                       ,clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_paid()                   as amount_type_cd
                                       ,sum(s.scc_loss_amt               )                   as amount
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s 
                                     ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                 union all
                                 select s.administrator
                                       ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                       ,clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_salvage()                as amount_type_cd
                                       ,sum(s.scc_salvage_subro_amt         )                as amount
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s 
                                     ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                 group by s.administrator
                                          ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                          ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                          ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                          ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                 union all
                                 select s.administrator
                                       ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                       ,clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_lae()                    as amount_type_cd
                                       ,sum(s.scc_expense_amt)                               as amount
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s 
                                      ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                 union all
                                 select s.administrator
                                       ,c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                       ,s.amount_type_cd
                                       ,sum(s.amount)                               as amount
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle  s 
                                      ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  amount_type_cd              <> clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                         ,s.amount_type_cd
                             )                                         x
                            ,clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd         lku
                       where 1                = 1
                        and  x.amount        <> 0
                        and  x.amount_type_cd = lku.amount_type_cd
                       group by  x.administrator  
                                ,x.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed   
                                ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                                ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                                ,x.reinsurer_cd
                                ,x.amount_type_cd
                       having sum((x.amount * lku.multiplier_scc)) <> 0
                 $$;
   ---------------------------------------------
   ---------------------------------------------
   select count(*) into v_count_current
   from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s 
       ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
   where 1                           = 1
    and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm;
   if v_count_current > 0 then 
      call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql); 
   end if;

      ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F190  verify clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined when 
   --       we do not have data for the current accounting period
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F190';
   v_sql       = $$  
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                   except
                       select x.administrator  
                             ,x.scc_close_yyyymm   
                             ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                             ,x.reinsurer_cd
                             ,x.amount_type_cd
                             ,(x.amount * lku.multiplier_scc)                                            as amount
                       from (
                                 select s.administrator 
                                       ,c.scc_close_yyyymm 
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr 
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd  
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd   
                                       ,clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()                   as amount_type_cd    
                                       ,round(cast(sum(scc_reserve_amt_money) as numeric),0) as amount 
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s   
                                     ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c  
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm_prior_month
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                 union all
                                 select s.administrator
                                       ,c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                       ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                       ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                       ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                       ,s.amount_type_cd
                                       ,sum(s.amount)                               as amount
                                 from clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle  s 
                                      ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
                                 where 1                           = 1
                                  and  amount_type_cd              <> clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                                 group by s.administrator
                                         ,c.scc_close_yyyymm
                                         ,s.tpa_claim_nbr
                                         ,s.cna_suffix_cd    
                                         ,s.reinsurer_cd
                                         ,s.amount_type_cd
                             )                                         x
                            ,clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd         lku
                       where 1                = 1
                        and  x.amount        <> 0
                        and  x.amount_type_cd = lku.amount_type_cd
                 $$;
   ---------------------------------------------
   ---------------------------------------------
   select count(*) into v_count_current
   from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in        s 
       ,clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_scc_close c
   where 1                           = 1
    and  s.scc_close_yyyymm_proposed = c.scc_close_yyyymm;
   if v_count_current = 0 then 
      call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql); 
   end if;

      ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F200  verify tpa_close_yyyymm is caculated correctly in clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F200';
   v_sql       = $$  
            select distinct id, tpa_ending_dt, tpa_close_yyyymm from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
       except
            select distinct id, tpa_ending_dt, clmscc_lku.f_yyyymm_from_date(tpa_ending_dt) from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- F205  verify scc_close_yyyymm_proposed is caculated correctly in clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'F205';
   v_sql       = $$ 
            select id, scc_close_yyyymm_proposed from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in
       except
            select tpa.id , clmscc_lku.f_month_add_from_yyyymm(tpa.tpa_close_yyyymm,bp.months_to_add_cna_booking)
            from clmscc_mgmt.scc_valid_tpa_in           tpa
                ,clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_booking_period  bp
            where 1                       = 1
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

 

   return;

   return;
 
end; 
$BODY$;

    OWNER TO dbadmin;

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_g000_verify_claim_list()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_g000_verify_claim_list();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_g000_verify_claim_list(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;
begin

   ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-08-30 | 01)retire G110
   ------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'G%';

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G100  verify claim list in table 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_list 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_list
                   except
                       select distinct
                              administrator
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                       from (
                                  select c.administrator
                                        ,c.tpa_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined         c
                                      ,clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer              x
                                  where 1               = 1
                                   and  c.administrator = x.administrator
                                   and  c.tpa_claim_nbr = x.tpa_claim_nbr
                                   and  c.cna_suffix_cd = x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  union
                                  select x.administrator
                                        ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg c
                                      ,clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer              x
                                  where 1               = 1
                                   and  c.cna_claim_nbr = x.cna_claim_nbr
                                   and  c.cna_suffix_cd = x.cna_suffix_cd
                            ) x
                       where 1 = 1
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G110  verify claim list using in 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined and 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg       
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select distinct
                              administrator
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                       from (
                                  select c.administrator
                                        ,c.tpa_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined         c
                                      ,clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer              x
                                  where 1               = 1
                                   and  c.administrator = x.administrator
                                   and  c.tpa_claim_nbr = x.tpa_claim_nbr
                                   and  c.cna_suffix_cd = x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  union
                                  select x.administrator
                                        ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                                        ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                                  from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg c
                                      ,clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer              x
                                  where 1               = 1
                                   and  c.cna_claim_nbr = x.cna_claim_nbr
                                   and  c.cna_suffix_cd = x.cna_suffix_cd
                            ) x
                       where 1 = 1
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_list
                 $$;
   ---call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G120 verify claim list in clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked                
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G120';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select distinct 
                              administrator
                            , tpa_claim_nbr
                            , cna_claim_nbr
                            , cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
                   except
                       select administrator
                            , tpa_claim_nbr
                            , cna_claim_nbr
                            , cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G130  verify claim list in clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle_stat_code          
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G130';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle_stat_code
                   except
                       select tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G140  verify claim list in clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg               
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G140';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_stg_in_act_stat_code_chg
                   except
                       select tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd 
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G150  verify claim list in clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer 
   --       using cclmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_itd_totals             
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G150';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select  x.administrator
                               ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                               ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                               ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                               ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                               ,a.amount_type_cd
                               ,a.ind_movement
                               ,a.ind_as_of
                               ,a.max_dollar_amount
                               ,a.ind_pennies
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer            x
                            ,clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd         a
                        where 1 = 1
                   except
                        select administrator
                             , tpa_claim_nbr
                             , cna_seq_nbr
                             , cna_claim_nbr
                             , cna_suffix_cd
                             , amount_type_cd
                             , ind_movement
                             , ind_as_of
                             , max_dollar_amount
                             , ind_pennies
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_itd_totals
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G160  verify claim list in clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_itd_totals 
   --       using clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer           
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G160';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select administrator
                             , tpa_claim_nbr
                             , cna_seq_nbr
                             , cna_claim_nbr
                             , cna_suffix_cd
                             , amount_type_cd
                             , ind_movement
                             , ind_as_of
                             , max_dollar_amount
                             , ind_pennies
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_itd_totals
                   except
                        select  x.administrator
                               ,x.tpa_claim_nbr
                               ,x.cna_seq_nbr
                               ,x.cna_claim_nbr
                               ,x.cna_suffix_cd
                               ,a.amount_type_cd
                               ,a.ind_movement
                               ,a.ind_as_of
                               ,a.max_dollar_amount
                               ,a.ind_pennies
                        from clmscc_mgmt.scc_act_claim_xfer            x
                            ,clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd         a
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G170  verify ind_cna_claim_found in 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined using 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_list          
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G170';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_suffix_cd
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                        where ind_cna_claim_found = true
                   except 
                        select administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_suffix_cd
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_list
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G180  verify ind_stat_code_found in 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined using 
   --       clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_stat_code              
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G180';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                        select administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_suffix_cd
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                        where ind_stat_code_found = true 
                   except 
                        select administrator, tpa_claim_nbr, cna_suffix_cd
                        from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_claim_stat_code
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G19 verify clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle is populated 
   --     correctly from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined 
   --     where clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined is on the 
   --     botton of the except
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G190';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle
                   except 
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                       where ind_cna_claim_found = false
                         or  ind_stat_code_found = false
                         or  ind_processed       = false
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- G200 verify clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle is populated 
   --      correctly from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined 
   --      where clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle is on the botton of the except 
      ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'G200';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount
                       from clmscc_staging.scc_tmp_tpa_combined
                       where ind_cna_claim_found = false
                         or  ind_stat_code_found = false
                         or  ind_processed       = false
                   except
                       select administrator
                             ,scc_close_yyyymm
                             ,tpa_claim_nbr
                             ,cna_suffix_cd
                             ,reinsurer_cd
                             ,amount_type_cd
                             ,amount
                       from clmscc_mgmt.scc_recycle
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
   
   
   
   
   return;
   
   
   

end; 
$BODY$;

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_h000_rtrim()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_h000_rtrim();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_h000_rtrim(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;
begin

 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'H%';

   
   
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

 
 
 
 
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H100 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.adjusting_location_cd does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where adjusting_location_cd <> rtrim(adjusting_location_cd)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H101 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.administrator does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------

                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where administrator <> rtrim(administrator)
                 $$;

   ------------------------------------------------------

                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H104 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.create_user does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H104';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where create_user <> rtrim(create_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H105 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.update_user does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H105';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where update_user <> rtrim(update_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H106 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator.administrator does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H106';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator where administrator <> rtrim(administrator)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H107 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator.administrator_name does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H107';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator where administrator_name <> rtrim(administrator_name)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H108 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator.create_user does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H108';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator where create_user <> rtrim(create_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H109 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator.update_user does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H109';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_administrator where update_user <> rtrim(update_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H110 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd.amount_type_cd does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd where amount_type_cd <> rtrim(amount_type_cd)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H111 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd.amount_type_cd_desc does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H111';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd where amount_type_cd_desc <> rtrim(amount_type_cd_desc)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H112 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd.cobol_pic does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'H112';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd where cobol_pic <> rtrim(cobol_pic)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- H113 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_amount_type_cd.max_dollar_amount_with_comma does not need a rtrim
   ------------------------------------------------------

    OWNER TO dbadmin;

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;
begin

 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'I%';

   
   
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
 
 
 
 
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I100 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.adjusting_location_cd does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where adjusting_location_cd <> ltrim(adjusting_location_cd)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I101 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.administrator does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I101';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where administrator <> ltrim(administrator)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I102 - verify clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd.adjusting_location_cd_desc does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I102';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_adjusting_location_cd where adjusting_location_cd_desc <> ltrim(adjusting_location_cd_desc)
                 $$;

   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I801 - verify clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log.verify_id_desc does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I801';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log where verify_id_desc <> ltrim(verify_id_desc)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I802 - verify clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log.create_user does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I802';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log where create_user <> ltrim(create_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- I803 - verify clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log.update_user does not need a ltrim
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'I803';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                    select * from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log where update_user <> ltrim(update_user)
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);
 
 
 
   return;

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim() TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim() TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim() TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_i000_ltrim() TO iicsuser;

-- PROCEDURE: clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes()

-- DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes();

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes(
	)
LANGUAGE 'plpgsql'
AS $BODY$
declare v_verify_id      varchar;
declare v_sql            varchar;
begin
 
 ------------------------------------------------
   -- Date       | Change
   ------------------------------------------------
   -- 2022-09-28 | 01) script written
   ------------------------------------------------

   ------------------------------------------------------
   ------------------------------------------------------
   delete from clmscc_verify.scc_verify_log
   where 1 = 1
   and verify_id like 'J%';

   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*
   --*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*-*

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- J100  Number of cna_claim_nbr and cna_suffix_cd with nonmatching stat codes
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'J100';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                      -- 4 count start  
                      select  cnt.cna_claim_nbr, cnt.cna_suffix_cd ,count(*) as nbr_rows
                      from (
                               -- 30 distinct start  
                               select  distinct 
                                       stat.company_cd              ,stat.cna_claim_nbr    ,stat.cna_suffix_cd             ,stat.policy_number  ,stat.policy_eff_dt_str ,stat.loss_dt_str
                                      ,stat.notice_dt_str           ,stat.premium_state_cd ,stat.product_responsibility_cd ,stat.policy_type_cd ,stat.major_line_cd     ,stat.subline_cd
                                      ,stat.cause_of_loss_cd        ,stat.catastrophe_cd   ,stat.rating_method_cd          ,stat.branch_cd      ,stat.producer_cd       ,stat.adjusting_location_cd
                                      ,stat.end_of_record_indicator ,stat.indemnity_medical_ind
                               from (
                                            --- 100 case reserves start  
                                            select distinct 
                                                   cr.company_cd    ,cr.cna_claim_nbr ,cr.cna_suffix_cd         ,cr.policy_number             ,cr.policy_eff_dt_str         
                                                  ,cr.loss_dt_str   ,cr.notice_dt_str ,cr.premium_state_cd      ,cr.product_responsibility_cd ,cr.policy_type_cd        
                                                  ,cr.major_line_cd ,cr.subline_cd    ,cr.cause_of_loss_cd      ,cr.catastrophe_cd            ,cr.rating_method_cd    
                                                  ,cr.branch_cd     ,cr.producer_cd   ,cr.adjusting_location_cd ,cr.end_of_record_indicator   ,cr.indemnity_medical_ind
                                                  ,0.00              as scc_loss_amt          
                                                  ,0.00              as scc_expense_amt             
                                                  ,0.00              as scc_salvage_subro_amt    
                                                  ,1.00              as scc_reserve_amt   
                                            from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked                                                                      cr
                                            join (select max(scc_close_yyyymm) as scc_close_yyyymm from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked  where 1 = 1) ap                     
                                                  on cr.scc_close_yyyymm = ap.scc_close_yyyymm
                                            where 1                = 1  and  cr.amount_type_cd = clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                                            --- 100 case reserves end  
                                            union all
                                            --- 200 paid loss start      
                                            select pl.company_cd    ,pl.cna_claim_nbr ,pl.cna_suffix_cd         ,pl.policy_number             ,pl.policy_eff_dt_str
                                                  ,pl.loss_dt_str   ,pl.notice_dt_str ,pl.premium_state_cd      ,pl.product_responsibility_cd ,pl.policy_type_cd        
                                                  ,pl.major_line_cd ,pl.subline_cd    ,pl.cause_of_loss_cd      ,pl.catastrophe_cd            ,pl.rating_method_cd   
                                                  ,pl.branch_cd     ,pl.producer_cd   ,pl.adjusting_location_cd ,pl.end_of_record_indicator   ,pl.indemnity_medical_ind
                                                  ,sum(pl.scc_loss_amt         )  as scc_loss_amt          
                                                  ,sum(pl.scc_expense_amt      )  as scc_expense_amt             
                                                  ,sum(pl.scc_salvage_subro_amt)  as scc_salvage_subro_amt  
                                                  ,1.00                           as scc_reserve_amt 
                                            from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked pl
                                            where 1                 = 1
                                             and  pl.amount_type_cd <> clmscc_lku.f_amount_type_cd_case()
                                            group by  pl.company_cd    ,pl.cna_claim_nbr ,pl.cna_suffix_cd         ,pl.policy_number             ,pl.policy_eff_dt_str
                                                     ,pl.loss_dt_str   ,pl.notice_dt_str ,pl.premium_state_cd      ,pl.product_responsibility_cd ,pl.policy_type_cd       
                                                     ,pl.major_line_cd ,pl.subline_cd    ,pl.cause_of_loss_cd      ,pl.catastrophe_cd            ,pl.rating_method_cd
                                                     ,pl.branch_cd     ,pl.producer_cd   ,pl.adjusting_location_cd ,pl.end_of_record_indicator   ,pl.indemnity_medical_ind
                                            having sum(pl.scc_loss_amt          )  <> 0.00     
                                               or  sum(pl.scc_expense_amt       )  <> 0.00          
                                               or  sum(pl.scc_salvage_subro_amt )  <> 0.00 
                                            -- 200 paid loss end        
                                    ) stat
                               where 1 = 1
                               -- 30 distinct end --
                           ) cnt
                      where 1 = 1
                      group by cnt.cna_claim_nbr, cnt.cna_suffix_cd
                      having count(*) > 1
                      -- 4 count end --
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   ------------------------------------------------------
   -- J110  Number of administrator, cna_suffix_cd and indemnity_medical_ind invalid combinations in booked table
   ------------------------------------------------------
   v_verify_id = 'J110';
   v_sql       = $$ 
                       select administrator, cna_suffix_cd, indemnity_medical_ind from clmscc_mgmt.scc_booked
                       except
                       select administrator, cna_suffix_cd, indemnity_medical_ind from clmscc_lku.scc_lku_tpa_coverage_cd
                 $$;
   call clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_insert_into_verify_log(v_verify_id,v_sql);

   
   
   
   
   return;
   
   
   

end; 
$BODY$;

ALTER PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes()
    OWNER TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes() TO PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes() TO clmscc_db_rw;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes() TO dbadmin;

GRANT EXECUTE ON PROCEDURE clmscc_verify.scc_verify_sp_verify_j000_verify_stat_codes() TO iicsuser;
